# ğŸ§  High-Level System Architecture

# 1ï¸âƒ£ Data Ingestion Layer

### Inputs:

* WhatsApp/Telegram exported chats
* Email logs
* Interaction timestamps
* Mentions, tags, replies
* Calendar events
* Synthetic datasets

### Processing:

* Parse into structured format:

  ```

    contact_id,
    timestamp,
    message_length,
    response_time,
    sentiment_score,
    topic,
    interaction_type
  }
  ```

We extract:

* Response time
* Conversation frequency
* Sentiment trend
* Initiative ratio (who starts conversations)
* Mentions of plans (â€œletâ€™s meetâ€, â€œcall tomorrowâ€)

---

# 2ï¸âƒ£ Behavioral Modeling Layer

This is where your project becomes intelligent.

We compute:

### ğŸ“Š Relationship Health Score (RHS)

Example formula:

```
RHS = w1(Frequency Score)
    + w2(Response Consistency)
    + w3(Sentiment Trend)
    + w4(Initiative Balance)
    + w5(Time Since Last Meaningful Interaction)
```

Each metric normalized (0â€“100).

---

### ğŸ” Detect Patterns:

* Increasing response delay
* One-sided conversations
* Declining sentiment
* Repeated â€œletâ€™s planâ€ but no execution
* Sudden silence

This layer uses:

* Time series analysis
* Rolling averages
* Simple anomaly detection
* Basic ML (optional)

# 3ï¸âƒ£ Relationship Intelligence Engine

This is the brain.

It categorizes relationships:

| Category  | Condition                    |
| --------- | ---------------------------- |
| Thriving  | High RHS + mutual initiative |
| Stable    | Moderate RHS                 |
| At Risk   | Declining trend              |
| Dormant   | No activity beyond threshold |
| One-Sided | Initiative imbalance         |

This transforms raw logs â†’ structured social intelligence.

---

# 4ï¸âƒ£ Decision Engine

Now we automate actions based on logic.

Example rules:

### If:

* â€œItâ€™s been a while â€” want to check in?â€

### If:

---

### If:

This is rule-based + LLM-assisted suggestion generation.

# 5ï¸âƒ£ Automation & Action Layer

# 6ï¸âƒ£ Feedback Loop (Important for Judges)

# ğŸ¥‡ SOLUTION 1: Relationship Health Intelligence Engine (RHIE)

### ğŸ’¡ Core Idea:

---

## ğŸ”¥ What Makes It Powerful

Instead of reminders, this system:

* Models **relationship decay**
* Detects **emotional drift**
* Predicts **future interaction drop**
* Triggers proactive repair actions

---

## ğŸ§  Architecture

### 1ï¸âƒ£ Data Layer

From chat logs extract:

* Frequency
* Response delay
* Sentiment trend
* Initiative ratio
* Topic clusters
* â€œIntent mentionsâ€ (plans, promises)

---

### 2ï¸âƒ£ Relationship Health Score (RHS)

```

0.25 * Interaction Frequency Score +
```
